Let a_1 = shift_sint8(p, 0).
Assume {
  Type: is_sint32(j) /\ is_sint32(m) /\ is_sint32(match_0) /\ is_sint32(n).
  (* Heap *)
  Type: (region(p.base) <= 0) /\ (region(t.base) <= 0) /\ linked(Malloc_0) /\
      sconst(Mchar_0).
  (* Pre-condition *)
  Have: valid_rd(Malloc_0, t, 1).
  (* Pre-condition *)
  Have: valid_rd(Malloc_0, p, 1).
  (* Pre-condition *)
  Have: valid_rw(Malloc_0, a, n).
  (* Pre-condition *)
  Have: valid_rw(Malloc_0, a_1, m).
  (* Pre-condition *)
  Have: separated(a, n, a_1, m).
  (* Pre-condition *)
  Have: 0 < n.
  (* Pre-condition *)
  Have: 0 < m.
  (* Invariant *)
  Have: (0 <= j) /\ (j <= m).
  (* Invariant *)
  Have: forall i : Z. ((0 <= i) -> ((i < j) ->
      (Mchar_0[shift_sint8(t, match_0 + i)] = Mchar_0[shift_sint8(p, i)]))).
  Have: m <= j.
}
Prove: P_string_same(Mchar_0, t, p, n, j, match_0).
